<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nachtegale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nahtagala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nahtagalǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nahtigalǭ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***nachtmerrie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nachtmerrie.html>nachtmerrie</a> (2004)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nachtmerie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nachtmere</i>, likened to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:merrie.html>merrie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> through folk etymology; the actual formation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nachtmare</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nacht.html>nacht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mare</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nachtmerrie.html>nachtmerrie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nachtmerries.html>nachtmerries</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nachtmerrie.html>nachtmerrietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">nightmare</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">bad dream</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ugly woman, witch</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:angstig.html>angstige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:droom.html>droom</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:angstdroom.html>angstdroom</a>

***nader.html

<p>An old comparative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i>, from which also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a></i> originates. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">near</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaar</a> (20042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fall, autumn (season after summer)
<ul><li><b>1698</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>Steven</a> Blankaart, <i>Den Neder-landschen herbarius <a href = vnd.unilang:ofte.html>ofte</a> kruid-boek <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamste.html>voornaamste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruiden.html>kruiden</a></i>, Jan ten <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>Hoorn</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://dbnl.nl/tekst/blan012nede01_01/blan012nede01_01_0379.php">463</a>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewas.html>gewas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> dry <a href = vnd.unilang:voeten.html>voeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> water, <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dikke.html>dikke</a>, geknoopte <a href = vnd.unilang:groene.html>groene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stam.html>stam</a>, sig in <a href = vnd.unilang:verscheiden.html>verscheide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:takken.html>takken</a> verdeelende, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> in '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaar</a></b> geelagtig <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a>.
<dl><dd>This crop grows up to three <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> high, above the water, with a thick, noded green <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a>, branching into several twigs, that yellows in <b>fall</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naleven.html>naleven</a> (23745)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">after, <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to, subsequent to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to live</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naleven.html>naleven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To observe, live by, respect a rule etc.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nakomen.html>nakomen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:respecteren.html>respecteren</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volgen.html>volgen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To live on, have an afterlife, be continued after one's own time
<dl><dd><i>Oudmodische kunststromingen <b><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></b> in maniërisme.</i>
<dl><dd><i>Old-fashioned artistic styles often live on long in mannerism.</i></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doorleven.html>doorleven</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">after, subsequent to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nachleben</i>.
